# ╚██████╔╝╚██████╔╝██║  ██║██║ ╚████║   ██║   ██║   ██║      ██║       ╚██████╔╝███████╗╚██████╔╝██████╔╝██║  ██║███████╗       ██║   ██║  ██║██║  ██║██████╔╝███████╗

# ██╔══██╗██║   ██║██║  ██║██║   ██║██╔══╝     ██║       ██╔═══╝ ██╔══██║██║╚██╗██║██╔══╝  ██║
# ██████╔╝╚██████╔╝██████╔╝╚██████╔╝███████╗   ██║       ██║     ██║  ██║██║ ╚████║███████╗███████╗

#grain
increase_grain_quantity = {
	is_shown = {
		grain_market_panel_quantity <= 1000000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_market_panel_quantity
				var:grain_market_panel_quantity < 1000000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_market_panel_quantity
				add = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_quantity = {
	is_shown = {
		grain_market_panel_quantity > 50000
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_market_panel_quantity
				var:grain_market_panel_quantity > 50000
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_market_panel_quantity
				subtract = 50000
			}
		}
	}
}

#grain
buy_grain_budget_panel_visible = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		gold_reserves > international_buy_grain_budget_panel
		stockpiling_grain_var_state < 9000000
		has_technology_researched = international_trade
	}
}

#grain
buy_grain_budget_panel = {
	effect = {
		add_treasury = {
			value = 0
			subtract = international_buy_grain_budget_panel
			#add = international_buy_grain_budget_panel
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = central_bank_historic_place
					is_capital = yes
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = stockpiling_grain_state_1
					add = owner.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		var:sell_limit_var_1 > 0

# ╚══════╝╚═╝     ╚═╝     ╚══════╝ ╚═════╝   ╚═╝       ╚═╝     ╚═╝╚══════╝╚═╝  ╚═╝

#grain
buy_grain_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price
				value = grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = grain_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_grain_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_1
				value  = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price
				value = scope:target.grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.grain_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = grain_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_grain_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_grain_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_grain_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.grain_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_grain_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#grain quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_1
				value  = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#grain price
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price
				value = grain_price
			}

			#grain price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = grain_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:grain_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = grain_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = grain_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_grain_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_grain_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_grain_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0 
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_grain_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_grain_var_state > player.var:grain_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_grain_market_panel
		player.var:grain_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0 
		player.var:grain_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_grain_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price
				value = coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = coal_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_coal_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_1
				value  = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price
				value = scope:target.coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.coal_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = coal_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_coal_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_coal_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_coal_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.coal_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_coal_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#coal quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_1
				value  = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#coal price
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price
				value = coal_price
			}

			#coal price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = coal_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:coal_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = coal_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = coal_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_coal_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_coal_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_coal_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_coal_var_state > player.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_coal_market_panel
		player.var:coal_contract_1_year = 0
		var:coal_release_status = 0 
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_coal_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_coal_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_coal_var_state > player.var:coal_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_coal_market_panel
		player.var:coal_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0 
		player.var:coal_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_coal_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				name = sell_oil_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_oil_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

####################################################################################################################################################
#####################################################################################################################################################
#dye
buy_dye_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price
				value = dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:dye_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = dye_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_dye_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#dye quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_1
				value  = var:dye_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#dye price
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price
				value = scope:target.dye_price
			}

			#dye price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = dye_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:dye_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.dye_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = dye_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_dye_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_dye_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

	effect = {

				value = value = scope:player_country.dye_price
			}

				name = dye_buy_price_by_price

					multiply = scope:player_country.dye_price

			# 	value = 1
			# }

			}

			}

			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.small_arms_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = small_arms_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_small_arms_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_small_arms_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}

			save_scope_as = target
		}

				name = small_arms_sell_1

			}

			#small_arms price

			}
		}
	}
}
buy_small_arms_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_small_arms_var_state > player.var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_small_arms_market_panel
		player.var:small_arms_contract_1_year = 0
		var:small_arms_release_status = 0 
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_small_arms_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_small_arms_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_small_arms_var_state > player.var:small_arms_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_small_arms_market_panel
		player.var:small_arms_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0 
		player.var:small_arms_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_small_arms_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				name = sell_manowars_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_manowars_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}
buy_manowars_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		not  = {
			infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		}
		stockpiling_manowars_var_state > player.var:manowars_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state_market_owner > buy_manowars_market_panel
		player.var:manowars_contract_1_year = 0
		var:manowars_release_status = 0 
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = buy_manowars_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}
sell_manowars_market_panel_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		# not  = {
		# 	infamy >= infamy_threshold:pariah
		# }
		player.stockpiling_manowars_var_state > player.var:manowars_market_panel_quantity
		money_supply_state > sell_manowars_market_panel
		player.var:manowars_contract_1_year = 0
		var:sell_limit_var_1 < sell_limit_var_0 
		player.var:manowars_release_status = 0
		any_scope_treaty = { 
			any_scope_article = {
				has_type = material_supply 
			}
		}  
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = sell_manowars_custom_tooltip
		}
	}
}

#ironclads
buy_ironclads_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#ironclads quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_sell_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#ironclads price
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_sell_price
				value = ironclads_price
			}

			#ironclads price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = ironclads_price
				}
			}
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = sell_ironclads_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#ironclads quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_buy_1
				value  = var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#ironclads price
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_buy_price
				value = scope:target.ironclads_price
			}

			#ironclads price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:target.ironclads_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = buy_ironclads_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_buy_ironclads_1
				target = prev
			}
		}

	}
}
sell_ironclads_market_panel = {
	effect = {
		root = {
			save_scope_as = target
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = player_country

		}
		##############

		scope:target = {
			#ironclads quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_buy_1
				value  = scope:player_country.var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
			}
			#ironclads price
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_buy_price
				value = value = scope:player_country.ironclads_price
			}

			#ironclads price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_buy_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = scope:player_country.var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = scope:player_country.ironclads_price
				}
			}
			#for on_action & gui
			# set_variable = {
			# 	name = buy_ironclads_1
			# 	value = 1
			# }
		}
		scope:player_country = {
			#ironclads quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_sell_1
				value  = var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
			}

			#ironclads price
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_sell_price
				value = ironclads_price
			}

			#ironclads price by quantity
			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_sell_price_by_price
				value = {
					add = var:ironclads_market_panel_quantity
					multiply = ironclads_price
				}
			}

			set_variable = {
				name = ironclads_contract_1_year
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = sell_ironclads_1
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = order_sell_ironclads_1
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

			set_variable = {
				name = trade_dinar_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

		effect = {
			set_variable = {
				name = trade_dinar_var
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}

		is_shown = {
			var:trade_dinar_var = 1
		}
	}

		}

release_ammunition_on = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ammunition_var
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
release_ammunition_off = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ammunition_var
			value = 0
		}

	}
}
release_ammunition_on_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:release_ammunition_var = 1
	}
}
release_ammunition_off_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:release_ammunition_var = 0
	}
}

#grain
#quatituy
increase_grain_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_quantity
		#var:grain_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_store_quantity
				#var:grain_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_quantity
		var:grain_store_quantity > 1000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_store_quantity
				var:grain_store_quantity > 1000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_grain_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_quantity
		grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_quantity
				grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_quantity
		var:grain_release_quantity > 1000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_quantity
				var:grain_release_quantity > 1000
				var:grain_store_status = 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
#time
increase_grain_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_month
		var:grain_store_month < 1000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_store_month
		var:grain_store_month > 12
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_store_month
				var:grain_store_month > 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_grain_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_month
		grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_grain_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = grain_release_month
		var:grain_release_month > 12
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = grain_release_month
				var:grain_release_month > 0
				var:grain_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = grain_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

default_grain = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_grain_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_grain_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:grain_release_status = 1
	}
}

set_grain_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:grain_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_grain_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_grain_var_1 < 1000000
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		var:grain_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_grain = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_grain_var_1
			value = grain_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month_fixe
			value = var:grain_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_grain_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_grain_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_grain_1
					multiplier = grain_store_for_modifier
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_grain_1
					multiplier = xxxxxxxxxxxxx
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_grain_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_grain_var_1
			value = grain_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_grain_1
					multiplier = grain_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_release_grain_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#grain_release_predicted < stockpiling_grain_var_state

		grain_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_grain_var_state
		var:grain_store_status = 0
		var:grain_release_status = 0
		var:grain_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_grain = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_var_1
			value = grain_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_month_fixe
			value = var:grain_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_release_quantity_1_year
			value = grain_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_grain_1
				remove_modifier = release_grain_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_grain_1
					multiplier = grain_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = grain_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_grain_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_wood_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_store_quantity
		#var:wood_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = wood_store_quantity
				#var:wood_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_wood_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_store_quantity
		var:wood_store_quantity > 1000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = wood_store_quantity
				var:wood_store_quantity > 1000
				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_wood_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = wood_release_quantity
		wood_release_predicted < stockpiling_wood_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = wood_release_quantity
				wood_release_predicted < stockpiling_wood_var_state
				var:wood_store_status = 0
				var:wood_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = wood_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

#####################################################################################################################################################
set_wood_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:wood_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_wood_1
				remove_modifier = store_wood_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_wood_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_wood_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_wood_var_1 < 1000000
		var:wood_store_status = 0
		var:wood_release_status = 0
		var:wood_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_wood = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_wood_var_1
			value = wood_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_store_month_fixe
			value = var:wood_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wood_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_wood_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_wood_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_wood_1
				remove_modifier = store_wood_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_wood_1
					multiplier = wood_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		var:wood_release_quantity > 0
	}

				remove_modifier = release_wood_1

				}

		}

			value = 0

				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_iron_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = iron_release_quantity
		var:iron_release_quantity > 1000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = iron_release_quantity
				var:iron_release_quantity > 1000
				var:iron_store_status = 0
				var:iron_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = iron_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

default_iron = {
	is_shown = {
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_iron_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:iron_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_iron_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:iron_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_iron_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:iron_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_iron_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_iron_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_iron_var_1 < 1000000
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
		var:iron_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_iron = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_iron_var_1
			value = iron_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month_fixe
			value = var:iron_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_iron_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_iron_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_iron_1
					multiplier = iron_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_iron_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_iron_var_1
			value = iron_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_iron_1
					multiplier = iron_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_release_iron_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#iron_release_predicted < stockpiling_iron_var_state

		iron_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_iron_var_state
		var:iron_store_status = 0
		var:iron_release_status = 0
		var:iron_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_iron = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_iron_var_1
			value = iron_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_month_fixe
			value = var:iron_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_release_quantity_1_year
			value = iron_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_iron_1
				remove_modifier = release_iron_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_iron_1
					multiplier = iron_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = iron_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_iron_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

		var:lead_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = lead_release_month
				var:lead_release_month > 0
				var:lead_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = lead_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

set_lead_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:lead_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_lead_var_1 < 1000000
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
		var:lead_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_lead = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_lead_var_1
			value = lead_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month_fixe
			value = var:lead_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_lead_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_lead_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_lead_1
					multiplier = lead_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_lead_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_lead_var_1
			value = lead_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}

set_release_lead_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#lead_release_predicted < stockpiling_lead_var_state

		lead_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_lead_var_state
		var:lead_store_status = 0
		var:lead_release_status = 0
		var:lead_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_lead = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_var_1
			value = lead_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_month_fixe
			value = var:lead_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_release_quantity_1_year
			value = lead_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_lead_1
				remove_modifier = release_lead_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_lead_1
					multiplier = lead_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = lead_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_lead_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_oil_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_store_quantity
		#var:oil_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_store_quantity
				#var:oil_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_oil_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_store_quantity
		var:oil_store_quantity > 1000
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_store_quantity
				var:oil_store_quantity > 1000
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = oil_release_quantity
		oil_release_predicted < stockpiling_oil_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:oil_store_status = 0
		var:oil_release_status = 0
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = oil_release_quantity
				oil_release_predicted < stockpiling_oil_var_state
				var:oil_store_status = 0
				var:oil_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = oil_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

			name = dye_store_month_fixe
			value = var:dye_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_dye_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_dye_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_dye_1
					multiplier = dye_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_dye_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_dye_var_1
			value = dye_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1

					name = store_dye_1

set_release_dye_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#dye_release_predicted < stockpiling_dye_var_state

		dye_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_dye_var_state
		var:dye_store_status = 0
		var:dye_release_status = 0
		var:dye_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_dye = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_var_1
			value = dye_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_month_fixe
			value = var:dye_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_release_quantity_1_year
			value = dye_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_dye_1
				remove_modifier = release_dye_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_dye_1
					multiplier = dye_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = dye_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_dye_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#silk
#quatituy
increase_silk_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = silk_store_quantity
		#var:silk_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:silk_store_status = 0
		var:silk_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silk_store_quantity
				#var:silk_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:silk_store_status = 0
				var:silk_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = silk_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_silk_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = silk_store_quantity
		var:silk_store_quantity > 1000
		var:silk_store_status = 0
		var:silk_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silk_store_quantity
				var:silk_store_quantity > 1000
				var:silk_store_status = 0
				var:silk_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = silk_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_silk_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = silk_release_quantity
		silk_release_predicted < stockpiling_silk_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:silk_store_status = 0
		var:silk_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silk_release_quantity
				silk_release_predicted < stockpiling_silk_var_state
				var:silk_store_status = 0
				var:silk_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = silk_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = silk_release_quantity
		var:silk_release_quantity > 1000
		var:silk_store_status = 0
		var:silk_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silk_release_quantity

				var:silk_store_status = 0
				var:silk_release_status = 0
			}

				name = silk_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}

set_silk_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:silk_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_silk_1
				remove_modifier = store_silk_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = silk_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = silk_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = silk_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = silk_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_silk_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = silk_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = silk_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}

					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
				remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_rubber_1
					multiplier = rubber_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_release_rubber_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#rubber_release_predicted < stockpiling_rubber_var_state

		rubber_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_rubber_var_state
		var:rubber_store_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_status = 0
		var:rubber_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_rubber = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_var_1
			value = rubber_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_month_fixe
			value = var:rubber_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_release_quantity_1_year
			value = rubber_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_rubber_1
				remove_modifier = release_rubber_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_rubber_1
					multiplier = rubber_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = rubber_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_rubber_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#ammunition
#quatituy
increase_ammunition_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
		#var:ammunition_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
				#var:ammunition_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
		var:ammunition_store_quantity > 1000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_store_quantity
				var:ammunition_store_quantity > 1000
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_ammunition_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
		ammunition_release_predicted < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
				ammunition_release_predicted < stockpiling_ammunition_var_state
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ammunition_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
		var:ammunition_release_quantity > 1000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ammunition_release_quantity
				var:ammunition_release_quantity > 1000
				var:ammunition_store_status = 0
				var:ammunition_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ammunition_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

default_ammunition = {
	is_shown = {
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_ammunition_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:ammunition_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_ammunition_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:ammunition_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_ammunition_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_ammunition_1
				remove_modifier = store_ammunition_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ammunition_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_ammunition_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_ammunition_var_1 < 1000000
		var:ammunition_store_status = 0
		var:ammunition_release_status = 0
		var:ammunition_store_quantity > 0
	}

			value = var:ammunition_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ammunition_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {

		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_ammunition_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_ammunition_1
				remove_modifier = store_ammunition_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_ammunition_1
					multiplier = ammunition_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				remove_modifier = release_small_arms_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_small_arms_1
					multiplier = small_arms_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = small_arms_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_small_arms_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

increase_artillery_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = artillery_store_quantity
		#var:artillery_store_quantity < 1000000
		var:artillery_store_status = 0
		var:artillery_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = artillery_store_quantity
				#var:artillery_store_quantity < 1000000
				var:artillery_store_status = 0
				var:artillery_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = artillery_store_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_artillery_quantity_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = artillery_store_quantity
		var:artillery_store_quantity > 1000
		var:artillery_store_status = 0
		var:artillery_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = artillery_store_quantity
				var:artillery_store_quantity > 1000
				var:artillery_store_status = 0
				var:artillery_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = artillery_store_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_artillery_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = artillery_release_quantity
		artillery_release_predicted < stockpiling_artillery_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:artillery_store_status = 0
		var:artillery_release_status = 0

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = artillery_release_quantity

				var:artillery_store_status = 0
				var:artillery_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = artillery_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

		var:artillery_release_status = 0
	}

	is_shown = {
		var:artillery_store_status = 1
	}

	is_shown = {
		var:artillery_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_artillery_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:artillery_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_artillery_1
				remove_modifier = store_artillery_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_artillery_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_artillery_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_artillery_var_1 < 1000000
		var:artillery_store_status = 0
		var:artillery_release_status = 0
		var:artillery_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_artillery = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_artillery_var_1
			value = artillery_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_month_fixe
			value = var:artillery_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_artillery_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_artillery_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_artillery_1
				remove_modifier = store_artillery_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_artillery_1
					multiplier = artillery_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_artillery_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_artillery_var_1
			value = artillery_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {

set_release_artillery_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#artillery_release_predicted < stockpiling_artillery_var_state

		artillery_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_artillery_var_state
		var:artillery_store_status = 0
		var:artillery_release_status = 0
		var:artillery_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_artillery = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_artillery_var_1
			value = artillery_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_month_fixe
			value = var:artillery_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_release_quantity_1_year
			value = artillery_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_artillery_1
				remove_modifier = release_artillery_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_artillery_1
					multiplier = artillery_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = artillery_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_artillery_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = aeroplanes_release_quantity
		aeroplanes_release_predicted < stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state #chose la plus importante du mod
		var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = aeroplanes_release_quantity
				aeroplanes_release_predicted < stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state
				var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
				var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_release_quantity
				add = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_aeroplanes_quantity_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = aeroplanes_release_quantity
		var:aeroplanes_release_quantity > 1000
		var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = aeroplanes_release_quantity
				var:aeroplanes_release_quantity > 1000
				var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
				var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = aeroplanes_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

#####################################################################################################################################################
default_aeroplanes = {
	is_shown = {
		var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
	}
}
store_aeroplanes_green_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:aeroplanes_store_status = 1
	}
}
release_aeroplanes_red_bar = {
	is_shown = {
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 1
	}
}
#####################################################################################################################################################
set_aeroplanes_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_aeroplanes_1
				remove_modifier = store_aeroplanes_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_aeroplanes_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_aeroplanes_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_1 < 1000000
		var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_aeroplanes = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_aeroplanes_var_1
			value = aeroplanes_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_month_fixe
			value = var:aeroplanes_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_aeroplanes_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_aeroplanes_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_aeroplanes_1
				remove_modifier = store_aeroplanes_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_aeroplanes_1
					multiplier = aeroplanes_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_aeroplanes_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_aeroplanes_var_1
			value = aeroplanes_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_aeroplanes_1
				remove_modifier = store_aeroplanes_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_aeroplanes_1
					multiplier = aeroplanes_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_release_aeroplanes_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#aeroplanes_release_predicted < stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state

		aeroplanes_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_aeroplanes_var_state
		var:aeroplanes_store_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_status = 0
		var:aeroplanes_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_aeroplanes = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_aeroplanes_var_1
			value = aeroplanes_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_month_fixe
			value = var:aeroplanes_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_release_quantity_1_year
			value = aeroplanes_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_aeroplanes_1
				remove_modifier = release_aeroplanes_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_aeroplanes_1
					multiplier = aeroplanes_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = aeroplanes_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_aeroplanes_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ironclads_release_quantity
		var:ironclads_release_quantity > 1000
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ironclads_release_quantity
				var:ironclads_release_quantity > 1000
				var:ironclads_store_status = 0
				var:ironclads_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ironclads_release_quantity
				subtract = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
#time
increase_ironclads_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ironclads_store_month
		var:ironclads_store_month < 1000000
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ironclads_store_month
				add = 12
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ironclads_month_store = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ironclads_store_month
		var:ironclads_store_month > 12
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ironclads_store_month
				var:ironclads_store_month > 0
				var:ironclads_release_status = 0
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ironclads_store_month
				subtract = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_ironclads_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ironclads_release_month
		ironclads_release_predicted < stockpiling_ironclads_var_state
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ironclads_release_month
				add = 6
			}
		}
	}
}
reduce_ironclads_month_release = {
	is_valid = {
		has_variable = ironclads_release_month
		var:ironclads_release_month > 12
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ironclads_release_month
				var:ironclads_release_month > 0
				var:ironclads_release_status = 0

			}
			change_variable = {
				name = ironclads_release_month
				subtract = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

set_ironclads_0 = {
	is_valid = {
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
	}
	effect = {
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_ironclads_1
				remove_modifier = store_ironclads_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ironclads_var_1
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_month
			value = 12
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_month
			value = 12
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_reset = yes 
	}
}
set_store_ironclads_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		stockpiling_ironclads_var_1 < 1000000
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
		var:ironclads_store_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_store_ironclads = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_ironclads_var_1
			value = ironclads_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_month_fixe
			value = var:ironclads_store_month
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		# every_scope_state = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		has_building = building_national_stockpile
		# 	}

		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_ironclads_0
		# 	}
		# 	activate_production_method = {
		# 		building_type = building_national_stockpile
		# 		production_method = pm_store_ironclads_1
		# 	}
		# }
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_ironclads_1
				remove_modifier = store_ironclads_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_ironclads_1
					multiplier = ironclads_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_store_ironclads_infinit = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = store_ironclads_var_1
			value = ironclads_store_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_month_fixe
			value = 9999
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_month
			value = 9999
		}

		#reset release
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_quantity
			value = 1000
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_store_0 = yes 
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = release_ironclads_1
				remove_modifier = store_ironclads_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = store_ironclads_1
					multiplier = ironclads_store_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
set_release_ironclads_enabled = {
	is_valid = {
		#ironclads_release_predicted < stockpiling_ironclads_var_state

		ironclads_release_predicted_no_limit < stockpiling_ironclads_var_state
		var:ironclads_store_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_status = 0
		var:ironclads_release_quantity > 0
	}
}
set_release_ironclads = {
	is_shown = {
	}
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ironclads_var_1
			value = ironclads_release_quantity_1_week
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_quantity
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_status
			value = 1
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_month_fixe
			value = var:ironclads_release_month
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_release_quantity_1_year
			value = ironclads_release_predicted
		}
		validate_national_stockpiles_production_methods_release_0 = yes
		every_scope_building = {
			if  = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_national_stockpile
				}
				remove_modifier = store_ironclads_1
				remove_modifier = release_ironclads_1
				add_modifier = {
					name = release_ironclads_1
					multiplier = ironclads_release_for_modifier
				}
			}
		}

		#reset store
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_status
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ironclads_store_quantity
			value = 1000
		}

		#test
		set_variable = {
			name = release_ironclads_time
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

#grain

grain_buy_on = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_grain_var
			value = 1
		}
	}
}
grain_sell_off = {
	effect = {
		set_variable = {
			name = trade_grain_var
			value = 0
		}

	}
}
grain_buy_on_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_grain_var = 1
	}
}
grain_sell_off_v = {
	is_shown = {
		var:trade_grain_var = 0
	}
}
